28 #define MAX_OUT_LEN 48
29 static int check(const struct TEST_VECTOR *test)
30 {
31     unsigned char out[MAX_OUT_LEN];
32     struct BLOCK_MODE_STATE ctx;
33     size_t total = 0, out_len;
34     struct BLOCK_STATE blk;
35     if (!prim_avail(test->cipher))
36         return 1;
37     ASSERT_SUCCESS(block_init(&blk, test->key, test->key_len, test->cipher, 0));
38     ASSERT_SUCCESS(block_mode_init(&ctx, &blk, test->iv, test->iv_len, 1,
39                                    BLOCK_MODE_OFB, 0));
40     block_mode_update(&ctx, &blk, test->in, test->in_len,
41                       out, &out_len);
42     total += out_len;
43     ASSERT_SUCCESS(block_mode_final(&ctx, &blk,  out + total, &out_len));
44     total += out_len;
45     ASSERT_EQ(total, test->out_len);
46     ASSERT_BUF_EQ(out, test->out, test->out_len);
47     total = 0;
48     ASSERT_SUCCESS(block_mode_init(&ctx, &blk, test->iv, test->iv_len, 0,
49                                    BLOCK_MODE_OFB, 0));
50     block_mode_update(&ctx, &blk, test->out, test->out_len,
51                       out, &out_len);
52     total += out_len;
53     ASSERT_SUCCESS(block_mode_final(&ctx, &blk, out + total, &out_len));
54     total += out_len;
55     ASSERT_EQ(total, test->in_len);
56     ASSERT_BUF_EQ(out, test->in, test->in_len);
57 
58     block_final(&blk);
59     return 1;
60 }
61 int test_vectors_ofb(void);
62 int test_vectors_ofb(void)
63 {

65     if (!prim_avail(BLOCK_MODE_OFB))
66         return 1;
67     for (t = 0; t < ARRAY_SIZE(tests); ++t)
68         if (!check(tests + t)) return 0;

9046 #define MAX_OUT_LEN 32
9047 static int check(const struct TEST_VECTOR *test)
9048 {
9049     unsigned char out[MAX_OUT_LEN];
9050     struct HASH_STATE state;
9051     ASSERT_SUCCESS(hash_init(&state, HASH_SHA256, 0));
9052     hash_update(&state, test->in, test->in_len);
9053     hash_final(&state, out);
9054 
9055     ASSERT_BUF_EQ(out, test->out, test->out_len);
9056 
    return 1;
9057 }
9058 int test_vectors_sha256(void);
9059 int test_vectors_sha256(void)
9060 {
9061     size_t t;
9062     if (!prim_avail(HASH_SHA256))
9063         return 1;
9064     for (t = 0; t < ARRAY_SIZE(tests); ++t)
9065         if (!check(tests + t)) return 0;
9066     return 1;
9067 }
